21/06/24, 11:59 am - +91 98071 13102: CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` FUNCTION `fine_call`(mem INT) RETURNS int
    DETERMINISTIC
BEGIN
    DECLARE dif INT;
    DECLARE fin INT;
    DECLARE var_isu DATE;
    DECLARE var_ret DATE;

    -- Select issue date and return date into variables
    SELECT issue_date, return_date INTO var_isu, var_ret
    FROM book_issue 
    WHERE mcode = mem;

    -- Calculate the difference in days between return date and issue date
    SET dif = DATEDIFF(var_ret, var_isu);

    -- If the difference is more than 7 days, calculate the fine
    IF dif > 7 THEN
        SET fin = (dif - 7) * 10;
    ELSE
        SET fin = 0;
    END IF;

    RETURN fin;
END

- Teams must consist of 6 members from the same college, including at least one female.

14/10/24, 11:49 am - Tanisha Idnani SCIT: Greetings SCIT students !

We are pleased to open applications at *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* for the *Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program*, an *online Live Project* that helps you gain work experience in *data-driven decision making*. 

*No pre-requisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of the program and all necessary *training* on data-driven decision-making & *Power BI* will be imparted on the program.

To apply, students can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch with them:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba_application?src=scitw

*Benefits* post completion: 
* *Certificate of Work Experience*
* *Letter of Recommendation*

The program will also have *live sessions* to cover additional business cases. 

*Program Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on student choice)

The program uses a *case study-driven approach*, where you will *assess business projects* and *solve problems* using models used by leading firms like *McKinsey*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on actual *sales data* to gain insights.

*Program Start*: Flexible on student choice. Can be started *post exams*. 

This project is running at *leading campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

*Time Commitment*: 2 - 4 hours per week

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 1999 + GST / 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*:  A *fee waiver of 15 - 25%* shall be given to all *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune*  students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1690 + GST / Rs. 2199 + GST. 

To be eligible for the fee waiver, kindly apply through the abovementioned link only.

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics

28/10/24, 10:44 am - Tanisha Idnani SCIT: Greetings SCIT students !

Please note that *tonight, 11;59pm* is the *deadline* to apply at *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* for the *Finlatics Business Analyst Experience Program*, an *online Live Project* that helps you gain work experience in *data-driven decision making*. 

*No pre-requisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of the program and all necessary *training* on data-driven decision-making & *Power BI* will be imparted on the program.

To apply, students can fill out the form below and we'll get in touch with them:

https://www.finlatics.com/ba_application?src=scitwd

*Benefits* post completion: 
* *Certificate of Work Experience*
* *Letter of Recommendation*

The program will also have *live sessions* to cover additional business cases. 

*Program Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on student choice)

The program uses a *case study-driven approach*, where you will *assess business projects* and *solve problems* using models used by leading firms like *McKinsey*. You'll also learn *Power BI*, a business intelligence tool, and use it on actual *sales data* to gain insights.

*Program Start*: Flexible on student choice. Can be started *post exams*. 

This project is running at *leading campuses* including *IIT Bombay, IIT Delhi, IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

*Time Commitment*: 2 - 4 hours per week

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee of Rs. 1999 + GST / 2999 + GST (on student choice)

*Fee Waiver*:  A *fee waiver of 15 - 25%* shall be given to all *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune*  students on the abovementioned minimal induction fee. This waiver will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1690 + GST / Rs. 2199 + GST. 

To be eligible for the fee waiver, kindly apply through the abovementioned link only.

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement. 

Best regards,
Team Finlatics

We are pleased to open applications at *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* for the *Finlatics Startup Strategist Experience Program*, an *online Live Project* that helps you gain *work experience* in *building, launching & scaling a start-up*.

On this project, you'll work on start-up ideas across sectors like *fintech, digital media & OTT* and *sustainable & consumer tech* to develop business models, launch & financing strategies. 

This project also runs at *IIT Bombay*, *IIT Delhi*, *IIT Madras* and *BITS Pilani* among others.

On completing, you'll get: 
- *Certificate of Work Experience*
- *Letter of Recommendation*

You can apply via the link below and we'll get in touch:

https://www.finlatics.com/ssep_application?src=scitw

*No prerequisites* or prior domain knowledge is required to be a part of this project. Training will be a part of the project itself. 

*Project Duration* : 1 month / 2 months (on your choice)

*Project Start*: Flexible on your schedule. 

You can also take a *break* for exams, assignments, or personal commitments and take an *extension* if you cannot complete it within the duration. 

If selected, the program has a minimal induction fee: Rs. 1999 + GST

*Fee Waiver* : A *fee waiver of 25%* shall be given to all *Symbiosis Centre for Information Technology, Pune* students on the abovementioned fee. This will *reduce the fee* to Rs. 1499 + GST. 

Looking forward to a fruitful engagement,

Team Finlatics

22/01/25, 8:11 pm - Ashvin SCIT: 🌍IIT Bombay | Entre-MUN 2025

Registration Form https://docs.google.com/forms/d/e/1FAIpQLScGbnaJVbl4icV5Ry8uswyJZDehZFehMf6AqKkMRIq1hFSllw/viewform

Our Website https://www.ecell.in/esummit/mun

Hi! 👋  
We’re excited to invite you to Entre-MUN, a dynamic Model United Nations simulation happening as part of E-Summit 2025—Asia’s largest entrepreneurship event!  

📅 Dates: 1st & 2nd February 2025  
📍 Venue: IIT Bombay  

🔍 What is Entre-MUN?  
Entre-MUN is an engaging simulation of the United Nations, where participants step into the roles of global leaders and diplomats to debate and solve real-world issues. It’s the perfect platform to develop your critical thinking, public speaking, and leadership skills while engaging in impactful discussions.  

✨ Why Should You Join?  
- Certificate of Participation from IIT Bombay and recognized United Nations bodies  
- Sharpen your diplomacy, negotiation, and communication skills  
- Collaborate with bright minds and industry leaders  
- Engage in meaningful debates and propose innovative solutions  

🍴 Two days of lunch and high tea are included in the registration fee!  

This is your chance to grow, lead, and make an impact! Feel free to reach out if you have any questions.  

Follow our insta page for more updates https://www.instagram.com/entremun.iitb/

Looking forward to seeing you at Entre-MUN 2025! 🚀

25/01/25, 11:02 am - Shaniya Joseph SCIT: **📣 Announcement: Alpha Battle Day -6 Timeline & Rules**  

Greetings, everyone!  
Here’s the official timeline and rules for **Day 6 of Alpha Battle**, featuring **Table Tennis** and **Dodgeball** matches. Let’s gear up for an action-packed day!  

---

 **1. TABLE TENNIS SINGLES (Men & Women)**  
📅 Date: **25th January**  
🕔 Start Time: **5:00 PM**  

**Rules for Singles Matches:**  
- **Participants:** One male and one female player from each division will represent in the singles category.  
- **Round Stage Format:** Matches will consist of **one set of 21 points**.  
- **Knockout Stage (Semis & Finals):** Held on **27th January**. Matches will consist of **3 sets of 21 points each**.  

**2. TABLE TENNIS DOUBLES & MIXED DOUBLES**  
📅 Date: **25th-26th January**  
**Rules for Doubles Matches:**  
- The format for round stage matches remains the same: **one set of 21 points**.  
- Knockout stage (Semis & Finals) will also be held on **27th January**, with **3 sets of 21 points each** per match.  

**Note:**  
- The same player can participate in both singles and doubles OR different players can represent their division, depending on the team strategy.  


**3. DODGEBALL (Mixed & Women’s Matches)**  
📅 Date: **25th January - 26th January**  
🕕 Tentative Start Time: **After 6:00 PM**  

**Mixed Matches**  
- **Team Size:** 7 players (4 boys, 3 girls).  

**Women’s Matches**  
- **Team Size:**  6 players.  

**Common Rules for All Dodgeball Matches:**  
1. **Elimination Rule:** When a player is hit by a thrown ball, that player is **eliminated**.  
2. **Circle Rule:** A maximum of **2 individuals** are allowed inside the circle at a time.  
3. **Recovery Rule:** Recovery will follow a **rotation-wise system**.  

**Match Format:**  
- **Duration:** One round of **15 minutes per match**.  
- The team that eliminates the maximum number of opposing players will be declared the winner.  

---

**📢 Important Reminders for All Sports:**  
1. All divisions **must form their respective teams** with their SportsComm representative by the **morning of the game day**.  
2. A **final team sheet** must be prepared and submitted before the match.  
3. Teams should be **present at least 5 minutes before their scheduled match time** to ensure smooth and energetic events.  
4. Let’s bring in the energy and **cheer for all teams** to make this day an amazing experience!  

Get ready to showcase your skills, teamwork, and sportsmanship! Let the Alpha Battle spirit shine! ✨  

All the best, everyone! 💪
